          jQuery('document').ready(function() {
    jQuery('#searchForm').submit(function() {
      var scp = jQuery('#Select1').val();      
      if(scp==='Local Directory') {
        var keyword = jQuery('#SearchText').val();
        window.location="http://akronohio.planetdiscover.com/sp?keywords=" + keyword + "&amp;skin=&amp;aff=1109&amp;Submit2=Go";        
        return false;
      }
    });   
  });

/* Add as home page script - Dave Goodman goodmangraphics.co.uk */
function addashomepage(){
	//Bring back the browser object
	jQuery.browser = {};
	//Rest all is self explanatory.
	jQuery.browser.mozilla = /mozilla/.test(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase())
						&amp;&amp; !/webkit/.test(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase());
	jQuery.browser.webkit = /webkit/.test(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase());
	jQuery.browser.opera = /opera/.test(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase());
	jQuery.browser.msie = /msie/.test(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase());
	//jQuery.browser.maxthon = /(lunascape|maxthon|netfront|jasmine|blazer)[\/\s]?((\d+)?[\w\.]+)*/i.test(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase());
	//jQuery.browser.maxthon = navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Maxthon") &gt; -1 &amp;&amp; jQuery.browser.webkit &amp;&amp; !window.chrome;
	//jQuery.browser.maxthon = (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Maxthon') != -1 &amp;&amp; navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Maxthon') == -1);
	//jQuery.browser.maxthon = !!navigator.userAgent.match(/Version\/[\d\.]+.*Maxthon/)
	//jQuery.browser.maxthon = /maxthon/.test(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase());
 
    // makes jQuery differentiate between Chrome and Safari - thanks to Vikrant Chaudhary
    jQuery.browser.chrome = jQuery.browser.webkit &amp;&amp; !!window.chrome;
    jQuery.browser.safari = jQuery.browser.webkit &amp;&amp; !window.chrome;
	//$.browser.opera  = /opera/.test(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase());
	//var Opera = (navigator.userAgent.match(/Opera|OPR\//) ? true : false);
	//var isOpera = Object.prototype.toString.call(window.opera) == '[object Opera]';
	
	var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
	var msie = ua.indexOf("MSIE ");
	
    if (jQuery.browser.msie) { // IE 
        if (jQuery.browser.msie  &amp;&amp; parseInt(jQuery.browser.version, 10) &lt; 8) { // IE is v7 or lower - use ye olde homepage code
            document.body.style.behavior='url(#default#homepage)';
            document.body.setHomePage(window.location.href);
        } else { // IE v8 or higher
            var homesettext = "&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Internet Explorer&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To set your homepage in Internet Explorer 9 or later:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol &gt;&lt;li&gt;Open the main internet tools menu in your browser. This will be called something like &lt;strong&gt;TOOLS, EDIT, FIREFOX or SAFARI&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Select the tab marked &lt;strong&gt;GENERAL, PREFERENCES, OPTIONS or INTERNET OPTIONS&lt;/strong&gt; (depending on your browser).&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Look for a box labeled &lt;strong&gt;HOMEPAGE, HOMEPAGE LOCATION&lt;/strong&gt; or something similar. Type &lt;em&gt;http://www.ohio.com/ &lt;/em&gt; into this box and click OK. Your new homepage will be set.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li style='list-style-type: none;'&gt;&lt;br&gt;If you need further help setting your homepage, check your browser's Help menu.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;";
        };
		//if (msie &gt; 0 || !!navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident.*rv\:11\./)) { // IE11
			//var homesettext = "&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Internet Explorer&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To set your homepage in Internet Explorer 9 or later:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol &gt;&lt;li&gt;Open the main internet tools menu in your browser. This will be called something like &lt;strong&gt;TOOLS, EDIT, FIREFOX or SAFARI&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Select the tab marked &lt;strong&gt;GENERAL, PREFERENCES, OPTIONS or INTERNET OPTIONS&lt;/strong&gt; (depending on your browser).&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Look for a box labeled &lt;strong&gt;HOMEPAGE, HOMEPAGE LOCATION&lt;/strong&gt; or something similar. Type &lt;em&gt;http://www.ohio.com/ &lt;/em&gt; into this box and click OK. Your new homepage will be set.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li style='list-style-type: none;'&gt;&lt;br&gt;If you need further help setting your homepage, check your browser's Help menu.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;";       
		//}
    } else if (msie &gt; 0 || !!navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident.*rv\:11\./)) { // IE11
		var homesettext = "&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Internet Explorer&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To set your homepage in Internet Explorer 9 or later:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol &gt;&lt;li&gt;Open the main internet tools menu in your browser. This will be called something like &lt;strong&gt;TOOLS, EDIT, FIREFOX or SAFARI&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Select the tab marked &lt;strong&gt;GENERAL, PREFERENCES, OPTIONS or INTERNET OPTIONS&lt;/strong&gt; (depending on your browser).&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Look for a box labeled &lt;strong&gt;HOMEPAGE, HOMEPAGE LOCATION&lt;/strong&gt; or something similar. Type &lt;em&gt;http://www.ohio.com/ &lt;/em&gt; into this box and click OK. Your new homepage will be set.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li style='list-style-type: none;'&gt;&lt;br&gt;If you need further help setting your homepage, check your browser's Help menu.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;";       
	
	} else if (navigator.userAgent.match(/maxthon/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/maxthon/i) ) { // maxthon
        var homesettext = "&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Maxthon&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To set your homepage in Maxthon:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt;&lt;li&gt;In the top-right corner of your window, click the Maxthon menu. From the drop-down menu that appears, select &lt;strong&gt;SETTINGS&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Under 'Open On Startup', select the &lt;strong&gt;Open a specific page or set of pages. Set pages&lt;/strong&gt; radial box.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Click the &lt;strong&gt;SET PAGES&lt;/strong&gt; text, type &lt;em&gt;http://www.ohio.com/ &lt;/em&gt;, in the text box, then click &lt;strong&gt;OK&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;";      
    
	} else if (jQuery.browser.safari) { // safari
        var homesettext = "&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Safari&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To set your homepage in Safari for Mac OS X or Microsoft Windows:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt;&lt;li&gt;Select the Safari gear icon at the top of your browser window. From the drop-down menu that appears, select &lt;strong&gt;PREFERENCES&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;At the top of the dialog box, select the &lt;strong&gt;GENERAL&lt;/strong&gt; tab.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;In the &lt;strong&gt;HOME PAGE&lt;/strong&gt; section, type &lt;em&gt;http://www.ohio.com/ &lt;/em&gt;, then click the red 'close' button.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;";       
 
    } else if (jQuery.browser.webkit) { // chrome
        var homesettext = "&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Chrome | Opera&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To set your homepage in Chrome or Opera:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style='color:#9e0a0a;'&gt;(Chrome)&lt;/span&gt; In the top-right corner of your window, click the Chrome menu.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style='color:#9e0a0a;'&gt;(Opera)&lt;/span&gt; In the top-left browser window click the Opera button.&lt;br /&gt; From the drop-down menu that appears, select &lt;strong&gt;SETTINGS&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Under 'On startup', select the &lt;strong&gt;Open a specific page or set of pages. Set pages&lt;/strong&gt; radial box.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Click the &lt;strong&gt;SET PAGES&lt;/strong&gt; text, type &lt;em&gt;http://www.ohio.com/ &lt;/em&gt;, in the text box, then click &lt;strong&gt;OK&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;";     
 
    } else if (jQuery.browser.mozilla) { // firefox
        var homesettext = "&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Mozilla Firefox&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To set your homepage in Firefox&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt;&lt;li&gt;In the &lt;strong&gt;TOOLS&lt;/strong&gt; menu, select &lt;strong&gt;OPTIONS&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;At the top of the dialog box, select the &lt;strong&gt;GENERAL&lt;/strong&gt; tab.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;In the &lt;strong&gt;HOME PAGE&lt;/strong&gt; text box, type &lt;em&gt;http://www.ohio.com/ &lt;/em&gt;, then click OK. &lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;";     
	
	} else if (jQuery.browser.opera) { // opera
        var homesettext = "&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Opera&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To set your homepage in Opera on Microsoft Windows:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt;&lt;li&gt;Navigate to and click on the 'Preferences' link from the drop-down menu at the top of the Opera browser. Select the 'General' tab.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Click on 'Set current page as home page'.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;strong&gt;OK&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;To set your homepage in Opera on Mac OS X:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt;&lt;li&gt;Click on the top menu option 'Opera,' and then click on the 'Preferences' option. 	} else { // unknown browser
        var homesettext = "&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Unknown browser type&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To set your homepage please refer to your browser's help&lt;/a&gt;";       
    };
 
    if (homesettext){
        $("#homepagePopup .set-text").html(homesettext);
		$("#homepagePopup-overlay").fadeIn();
        $("#homepagePopup").fadeIn();
		$("#homepagePopup").draggable({containment: "self"});
    };
 
};

        function HiLo(data, status) {
            var wdata = data.d.split("|");
            //Hi Temp
            // 2015 CHANGE HERE jQuery('#currentHigh').text("High: " + Math.round(wdata[0]) + "\u00B0");
            //Low Temp

        function WidgetWeather(data, status) {
            var adata = new Array;
            var wdata = "";
            var conditions = "";
            //alert(status);
            //alert(data.d);
            wdata = data.d;
            adata = wdata.split("|");

            //Current Temp F
            jQuery('#currentTemp').text(Math.round(adata[3]) + "\u00B0");
            //Current Icon and conditions
            
            //Current Temp F
            jQuery('#currentTemp-mobile').text(Math.round(adata[3]) + "\u00B0");
            //Current Icon and conditions
            
            //Current Temp F
            jQuery('#currentTemp-mobile').text(Math.round(adata[3]) + "\u00B0");
            //Current Icon and conditions

            // 2015 CHANGE HERE conditions = "Current conditions: " + adata[2] + " Winds: From " + adata[6] + " @ " + Math.round(adata[8]) + " mph, Gusting: " + Math.round(adata[9]) + " mph, Humidity: " + adata[5] + "%" + ", Dew point: " + Math.round(adata[10]) + "\u00B0" + "F";
            // 2015 CHANGE HERE jQuery('#conditionsIcon').append("&lt;img src='" + "/img/akron/weather/fcicons/" + adata[15].replace("jpg", "png") + "' title='" + conditions + "'/&gt;");
            //Wind chill
            //if (adata[12] == '') { adata[12] = Math.round(adata[3]) }; //No wind chill use current temp.
            //jQuery('div.current_windchill').text('Wind chill: ' + adata[12] + "\u00B0" + "F" + " Gusting: " + Math.round(adata[9]) + " mph");
            
            // 2015 CHANGE HERE conditions = "Current conditions: " + adata[2] + " Winds: From " + adata[6] + " @ " + Math.round(adata[8]) + " mph, Gusting: " + Math.round(adata[9]) + " mph, Humidity: " + adata[5] + "%" + ", Dew point: " + Math.round(adata[10]) + "\u00B0" + "F";
            // 2015 CHANGE HERE jQuery('#conditionsIcon-mobile').append("&lt;img src='" + "/img/akron/weather/fcicons/" + adata[15].replace("jpg", "png") + "' title='" + conditions + "'/&gt;");
            //Wind chill
            //if (adata[12] == '') { adata[12] = Math.round(adata[3]) }; //No wind chill use current temp.
            //jQuery('div.current_windchill').text('Wind chill: ' + adata[12] + "\u00B0" + "F" + " Gusting: " + Math.round(adata[9]) + " mph");


        }

        function GetAlerts(data, status) {
            //alert(data.d);
            var adata = data.d.split("||");
            var acount = adata.length - 1;
            var afields = new Array;
            var severitycolor = "";
           
            if (acount != 0) { $("#currentAlert").append("&lt;a href='http://www4.thebeaconjournal.com/NOAAweatherdata/weather_sample5.html#page=page-3'&gt;&lt;b&gt;Weather Warning&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;") };
            
        }
        
        function OnError(request, status, error) {
            //alert("Request: " + request + " Status: " + status + " Error: " + error);
        }

                  <script type="text/javascript">
                   var curImage = 1

var totalPics = 15;

function changePic(nextImage){
    if(nextImage == 0)
    nextImage = totalPics;

    if(nextImage &gt; totalPics)
    nextImage = 1;
  
    document.getElementById('myCapture').id = 'myCapture' +curImage;
    var nextMyCapture ='myCapture'+nextImage;
    document.getElementById(nextMyCapture).id = 'myCapture' ; 
  
    document.getElementById('photo' + curImage).style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById('photo' + nextImage).style.display = "block";
    var photoCount = nextImage + " / " + totalPics;
    document.getElementById('nav_buttons_pup_count').innerHTML = photoCount;
    curImage = nextImage; 
     //document.getElementById("adIframe").src=document.getElementById("adIframe").src;
     doPageView();
     refreshSlot();
     display_more();
}


function display_more(){
    jQuery('#left_photo').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#gallery-body-overlay').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.page-shadow-wide-wrapper').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.line-seperator-solid').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#gallery_content').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#side_caption_tools').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.tools-for-story').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_ad').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_tools').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#photo_area').find('#side_caption_tools').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.button-count-wrapper').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.navigation-button-wrapper').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#close_more').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#ad_placement').addClass('display_more');
    
    for( var i=0; i &lt; 54; i++) {
        jQuery('#photobox'+i +'').addClass('display_more');
    }
    jQuery('.photo_caption_container').each(function(){
         jQuery(this).addClass('display_more'); 
    });
    jQuery('#ad_placement').show();
    
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_tools').each(function() {
        jQuery('#side_caption_tools').addClass('display_more');
    });
}

function display_less(){
    jQuery('#left_photo').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#gallery-body-overlay').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.page-shadow-wide-wrapper').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.line-seperator-solid').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#gallery_content').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#side_caption_tools').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.tools-for-story').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('div[id="#side_caption"]').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_ad').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_tools').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#photo_area').find('#side_caption_tools').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.button-count-wrapper').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.navigation-button-wrapper').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#close_more').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#ad_placement').removeClass('display_more');

    for( var i=0; i &lt; 54; i++) {
        jQuery('#photobox'+i +'').removeClass('display_more');
    }
    jQuery('.photo_caption_container').each(function(){
         jQuery(this).removeClass('display_more'); 
    });
    jQuery('#ad_placement').hide();
    
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_tools').each(function() {
        jQuery('#side_caption_tools').removeClass('display_more');
    });
}

function doPageView() {
    var filename = document.getElementById('myCapture' ).src;
    filename = filename.replace(/^.*[\\\/]/, '');
    pageName = window.location.pathname + "-" + filename;
    ga('send', 'pageview', {
        'page': pageName
    });
    //_gaq.push(['_trackPageview', pageName]);
}


var refreshSlot = function() {
googletag.cmd.push(function() {
googletag.pubads().refresh([gptAdSlots[0]]);
});
};
                  </script>

              <script type="text/javascript">
               function display_more(){
    jQuery('#left_photo').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#gallery-body-overlay').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.page-shadow-wide-wrapper').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.line-seperator-solid').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#gallery_content').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#side_caption_tools').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.tools-for-story').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_ad').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_tools').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#photo_area').find('#side_caption_tools').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.button-count-wrapper').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.navigation-button-wrapper').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#close_more').addClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#ad_placement').addClass('display_more');
    
    for( var i=0; i &lt; 150; i++) {
        jQuery('#photobox'+i +'').addClass('display_more');
    }
    jQuery('.photo_caption_container').each(function(){
         jQuery(this).addClass('display_more'); 
    });
    jQuery('#ad_placement').show();
    
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_tools').each(function() {
        jQuery('#side_caption_tools').addClass('display_more');
    });
}

function display_less(){
    jQuery('#left_photo').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#gallery-body-overlay').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.page-shadow-wide-wrapper').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.line-seperator-solid').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#gallery_content').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#side_caption_tools').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.tools-for-story').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('div[id="#side_caption"]').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_ad').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_tools').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#photo_area').find('#side_caption_tools').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.button-count-wrapper').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('.navigation-button-wrapper').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#close_more').removeClass('display_more');
    jQuery('#ad_placement').removeClass('display_more');

    for( var i=0; i &lt; 150; i++) {
        jQuery('#photobox'+i +'').removeClass('display_more');
    }
    jQuery('.photo_caption_container').each(function(){
         jQuery(this).removeClass('display_more'); 
    });
    jQuery('#ad_placement').hide();
    
    jQuery('#left_photo').find('#side_caption_tools').each(function() {
        jQuery('#side_caption_tools').removeClass('display_more');
    });
}
              </script>

 function downloadJSAtOnload() {

   element.id = "_nw2e-js";
 document.body.appendChild(element);

 if (window.addEventListener)
   window.addEventListener("load", downloadJSAtOnload, false);

     <!--END INSERT DEFER FOR LOADING VIDEOS-->
     <script type="text/javascript">
      function deferLoadingScript(url, callback) {
    var loadScript = function() {
        var s = document.createElement('script');
        s.type = 'text/javascript';
        s.src = url;

        if (typeof(callback) === 'function') {
            s.onload = s.onreadystatechange = function(event) {
                event = event || window.event;
                if (event.type === "load" || (/loaded|complete/.test(s.readyState))) {
                    s.onload = s.onreadystatechange = null;
                    callback();
                }
            };
        }

        document.body.appendChild(s);
    };

    window.addEventListener ? window.addEventListener('load', loadScript) : window.attachEvent('onload', loadScript);
}

/* Defer loading of some JS */
deferLoadingScript('http://launch.newsinc.com/js/embed.js');
     </script>

  <!-- START SCRIPT TO MAKE MENU SLIDE WORK -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   // 2015 Ohio.com menu replacement written by Charles Millard
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $('.slide-menu-trigger').click( function () {
            $('#slide-panel-main').css('visibility','visible');
            $('.slide-navigation-panel').toggleClass('isOpen');
            $('.slide-content-wrapper').toggleClass('pushed');
            //$(this).toggleClass('hide-trigger');
        });

        $('.openSubPanel').click( function() {
            $(this).next('.subPanel').addClass('isOpen');   
        });

        $('.closeSubPanel').click( function() {
            $(this).closest('.subPanel').removeClass('isOpen');
        });

        $('.closePanel').click( function() {
            $('#slide-panel-main').css('visibility','hidden');
            $('.slide-navigation-panel').removeClass('isOpen');
            $('.slide-content-wrapper').removeClass('pushed');
            $('.subPanel').removeClass('isOpen');
        });
            
        //$('.slide-content-container').click( function() {
            //$('.slide-navigation-panel').removeClass('isOpen');
            //$('.slide-content-wrapper').removeClass('pushed');
            //$('.subPanel').removeClass('isOpen');
        //});
        
        $('.slide-content-wrapper').click(function (event) {
            var selectSlideTrigger = $(event.target);
            selectSlideTrigger = selectSlideTrigger['context']; // context : clicked element inside body
            if ($(selectSlideTrigger).attr('id') != "slide-menu-tigger-button" &amp;&amp; $('#slide-panel-main').is(':visible') == true) {
                $('#slide-panel-main').css('visibility','hidden');
                $('.slide-navigation-panel').removeClass('isOpen');
                $('.slide-content-wrapper').removeClass('pushed');
                $('.subPanel').removeClass('isOpen');
                //$('#search-bar-content-wrapper').slideToggle(300);
            }
        });
        // Makes the search show in menu
        $('#show-search-bar').click(function() {
            $('#search-bar-content-wrapper').slideToggle(300);
         });
        // Resize window sets height of menu 100% to content
        function resizePanel(){
            $('#slide-panel-main').css("height", $(document).height());
        }
        $(window).resize(function(){
            resizePanel(); 
        });
        $(document).scroll(function(){
            resizePanel(); 
        });
        //initial call
        resizePanel();
    });
  </script>
  <!-- END SCRIPT TO MAKE MENU SLIDE WORK -->

    _sf_async_config.useCanonical = true;

    (function(){
      function loadChartbeat() {
        window._sf_endpt=(new Date()).getTime();
        var e = document.createElement('script');
        e.setAttribute('language', 'javascript');
        e.setAttribute('type', 'text/javascript');
        e.setAttribute('src', '//static.chartbeat.com/js/chartbeat_video.js');
        // removed for video tracking e.setAttribute('src', '//static.chartbeat.com/js/chartbeat_pub.js');
        //e.setAttribute('src', '//static.chartbeat.com/js/chartbeat.js');
        document.body.appendChild(e);
      }
      /** TELL CHARTBEAT TO AUTODETECT YOUTUBE VIDEOS **/
      var _cbv = window._cbv || (window._cbv = []);
      _cbv.push(['autoDetectYouTubeIframes']);
      var oldonload = document.ready;
      document.ready = (typeof document.ready != 'function') ?
         loadChartbeat : function() { oldonload(); loadChartbeat(); };
    })();
  </script>
